***proloog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:proloog.html>proloog</a> (41684)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prologus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πρόλογος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prólogos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:proloog.html>proloog</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:proloog.html>prologen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:proloog.html>proloogje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">prologue</span></li>
<li>first <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a> of a multi-stage cycling race like the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tour_de_France" class="extiw" title="w:Tour de France">Tour <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> France</a>.</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(taalkunde)</span> inleidende <a href = vnd.unilang:rede.html>rede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tekst.html>tekst</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:voorwoord.html>voorwoord</a>.</li>

***promotor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:promotor.html>promotor</a> (30298)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">promote</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-or</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:promotor.html>promotor</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:promotors.html>promotors</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(academia) A full <a href = vnd.unilang:professor.html>professor</a> of a Dutch, Flanders, South African, or German university who <a href = vnd.unilang:acts.html>acts</a> as the principal supervisor of a student's doctoral research.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A material that accelerates the action of a catalyst.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pronkstuk.html>pronkstuk</a> (41682)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pronken.html>pronken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to display</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuk.html>stuk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">piece</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>showpiece, centerpiece</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> prize, gem, jewel</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***prothese.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:prothese.html>prothese</a> (33106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prothesis</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:prothese.html>Prothese</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:prothese.html>prothese</a></i> and (now more common) <span class="Latn" lang="en">prosthesis</span> and French <span class="Latn" lang="fr">prothèse</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prothese.html>prothese</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prothesen.html>prothesen</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:protheses.html>protheses</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prothese.html>prothesetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The act of artificially <span class="Latn" lang="en">replacing</span> a <span class="Latn" lang="en">body part</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">prosthesis</span>, the artificial <span class="Latn" lang="en">replacement</span> for a body part</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">linguistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The addition of sound(s) at the beginning of a word after blurring of its semantics</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">by body part</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">heupprothese</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tandprothese</span> etc.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">these</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">thesis</span></li></ul>

</p>

***provincie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:provincie.html>provincie</a> (8749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:provincie.html>provincie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prōvincia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">territory <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>brought</a> under Roman domination; official duty, office, charge, province</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*prōw-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">right judge, master</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍆𐍂𐌰𐌿𐌾𐌰</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">frauja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lord, master</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">frēa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ruler, lord, king, master</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***provocateur.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:provocateur.html>provocateur</a> (100929)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:provocateur.html>provocateur</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">provocator</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:provocateur.html>provocateur</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:provocateurs.html>provocateurs</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who engages in provocative behavior.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  February 28,  “Daniel J. Wakin”, in  <cite>City <a href = vnd.unilang:opera.html>Opera</a> Lures Director From Paris</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2007/02/28/arts/music/28oper.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Gerard <a href = vnd.unilang:mortier.html>Mortier</a>, an iconoclastic <a href = vnd.unilang:impresario.html>impresario</a> and one of the <a href = vnd.unilang:opera.html>opera</a> world’s premier <b><a href = vnd.unilang:provocateurs.html>provocateurs</a></b>, will become general manager and artistic director of the New York City <a href = vnd.unilang:opera.html>Opera</a> in 2009.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>An <a href = vnd.unilang:undercover.html>undercover</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> who incites suspected persons to partake in or commit criminal <a href = vnd.unilang:acts.html>acts</a>.</li></ol>

***pruim.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pruim.html>pruim</a> (21821)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">prume</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*prūma</i>. A variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*plūma</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*plūmā</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prūnum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">προῦμνον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proûmnon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Plums.jpg/250px-Plums.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="206" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Plums.jpg/375px-Plums.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6c/Plums.jpg/500px-Plums.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="844" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i>Japanse <a href = vnd.unilang:pruim.html>pruim</a></i><br />Japanese plum</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruim.html>pruim</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pruimpje.html>pruimpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A plum tree, one of certain trees of the genus <i>Prunus</i>, especially <i>Prunus domestica</i>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">pruimenboom</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A plum <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fruit from a plum tree</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.
<ul><li>Hieronymus <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Alphen, "<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> pruimeboom".
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eieren.html>eieren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a>. / '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheen.html>Scheen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wou.html>wou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plukken.html>plukken</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:schoon.html>schoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vader.html>vader</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verbood.html>verbood</a>.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Little Jan once saw <b>plums</b> (or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:vulva.html>vulvas</a></b>; see below) hanging / <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a>! so big as eggs. / it seemed that little Jan <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> going to pluck them / though his father forbade him that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>John <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>'Mill (<a href = vnd.unilang:johan.html>Johan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> Meulen), "Pruimejantje".
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pruimen.html>pruimen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eieren.html>eieren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:groot.html>groot</a>; / <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tuinman.html>tuinman</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zag.html>zag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bolle.html>bolle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wangen.html>wangen</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:sloeg.html>Sloeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vuile.html>vuile</a> gapper <a href = vnd.unilang:dood.html>dood</a>.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">quid</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">piece of chewing tobacco</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">somewhat vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:vulva.html>vulva</a></li></ol>

<p>Compare regional <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Prüll</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stuff, junk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>No <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> than the late eighteenth century. From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prul.html>prul</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-aria</i>. It seems to have originally meant “literary dross”.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:prut.html>prut</a> (26513)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic, presumably a metonym from the sound made by a substance or something falling into it. First attested in early modern Dutch. The same in regional <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Prütt</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:prut.html>prut</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Sound of a thick, almost-solid substance.</span></li>
<li>cheers
<ul><li><b>2016</b> April 30, Wouter <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Noort, "‘<a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:twee.html>twee</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:banen.html>banen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doe.html>doe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a>’", <i>NRC Handelsblad</i>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:ondanks.html>Ondanks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> 27 <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verenigde.html>Verenigde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staten.html>Staten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hoor.html>hoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steeds.html>steeds</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a> Rotterdams <a href = vnd.unilang:accent.html>accent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maart.html>Maarten</a> Sierhuis. <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:biertje.html>biertje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zonnige.html>zonnige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terras.html>terras</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naast.html>naast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kantoor.html>kantoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:middenin.html>middenin</a> San Francisco <a href = vnd.unilang:proost.html>proost</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zegt.html>zegt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> „<b><a href = vnd.unilang:prut.html>Prut</a></b>!”</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>Any substance with a thick, gooey or almost-solid consistency, such as:

***psychiatrisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:psychiatrisch.html>psychiatrisch</a> (14203)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:psychiatrisch.html>psychiatrisch</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:psychiater.html>psychiater</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-isch</i>.
</p>
